  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9cf23019-d3d7-44c3-b559-e2f2950e6b27'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer6389316477686542399">Zoe is used to taking care of herself and has long ago accepted that if anything bad was going to happen, it was going to happen to her.   <span id="freeText6389316477686542399" style="display:none">Zoe is used to taking care of herself and has long ago accepted that if anything bad was going to happen, it was going to happen to her. So when she loses her job over something most bosses would probably be happy with and her life starts going down hill from there she doesn't expect it to get any better. She certainly didn't expect any help from the loud jerk next door, but then again she has nothing to lose so puts her trust in him and hopes for the best. What she didn't expect was the once in a lifetime opportunity that he offers her through an arrangement where they both benefit and no one is supposed to get hurt, but she should have known better because her luck has never been that good.<br /><br />Like most Bradfords, Trevor has a soft spot for food, but that's about all. He leads a pretty straightforward life and likes to keep things simple and that includes his relationships. He wants the perfect woman and knows exactly what she'll be like. So when he discovers much to his horror that he's thinking about his frumpy little neighbor he decides the best way to get his head straight is by working her out of his system. He'll keep her around, but only until he finds perfection.</span>

<div id="review_283679410" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/283679410" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5238046-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548068787p2/5238046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/283679410?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/5238046-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5238046-samantha?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5238046-samantha?shelf=0-kindle-book">0-kindle-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283679410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11415270795255812780">Meet Trevor, he's a jerk. He's looking for a dream woman he can flaunt around town and rub in other men's faces. Aside from being drop dead gorgeous, dream woman must also be a gourmet cook, come from a large family, and basically be willing to be Trevor's love puppet. Meet Zoe, Trevor's slightly over-weight and plain looking neighbor. Zoe is not having a good day. She just lost her job after exposing that one of the owner's wives was stealing money, her car's window broke, her obnoxious neighbo</span>
  <span id="freeText11415270795255812780" style="display:none">Meet Trevor, he's a jerk. He's looking for a dream woman he can flaunt around town and rub in other men's faces. Aside from being drop dead gorgeous, dream woman must also be a gourmet cook, come from a large family, and basically be willing to be Trevor's love puppet. Meet Zoe, Trevor's slightly over-weight and plain looking neighbor. Zoe is not having a good day. She just lost her job after exposing that one of the owner's wives was stealing money, her car's window broke, her obnoxious neighbor took up both her and his parking spots forcing her to park on the street. He then proceeded to use the last of her laundry detergent after tossing her clothes off of the communal washing machine and, to top it all off, confiscated her pizza. Having enough of being walked over that day, Zoe tries to reclaim her food only to have Trevor tell her "Its not like you need it." Feeling mildly guilty for saying that out loud, Trevor decides to make amends by getting Zoe a job at his uncle's construction business. He also decides to pay her to do his laundry, grocery shopping, and clean his apartment. Slowly over the weeks, Trevor and Zoe find themselves becoming friends. However, Trevor is mortified when he finds himself attracted to Zoe. After all, she's the complete opposite of his dream woman. She's plain, can't cook, and worst of all (to him) she's fat. Thinking it's just a phase that he'll eventually get over, Trevor proposes a friends with benefits relationship.<br /><br />I loathed Trevor in this book, to me, he had no redeeming qualities. The only reason why I didn't stop reading is because I enjoyed the first book in the series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11381643.Playing_for_Keeps__A_Neighbor_from_Hell___1_" title="Playing for Keeps (A Neighbor from Hell, #1) by R.L. Mathewson" rel="nofollow noopener">Playing for Keeps</a>, so I kept hoping that Mathewson would somehow save the book... but it never happened.<br /><br />Trevor's demeanor is supposed to come off as humorous and endearing, as in "Oh ha-ha, he has no regard for other people's feelings except his own. Oh tee-hee, he thinks everyone around him should be grateful for anything he does while he completely ignores all the things others do for him." This did not work for me. Trevor thinks he's god's gift to women and that Zoe should be grateful he's even deigning to talk to her because she's not up to his normal exacting standards. For her part, Zoe does everything for him except assist him in the bathroom and instead of acknowledging all that she does, Trevor completely writes it off as his due. Yes, he's paying her to clean his apartment and get his groceries, but what she does for him extends well beyond that. Somehow this attitude is supposed to come off as endearing and cute, but it just worked to frustrate me. Especially at the end, when Trevor begins to show some character growth by thinking that maybe he's been taking Zoe for granted. Of course that immediately goes down the drain when two seconds later he basically thinks, "Screw that! How dare she not believe I really want to be with her?!" Trevor is just an awful human being.<br /><br />And oh my god, the body hate in this book! There are so many malicious throw-away comments about Zoe and her weight that I lost count. Even Trevor hops on this band wagon by constantly thinking Zoe is too fat to be with him. In fact, he goes out of the way to avoid associating with her in public, even in a friendly sense, all she gets is an aloof head nod when they see each other. Trevor also constantly hears people saying disparaging things about her and just shrugs it off. Like, "yup, she's fat. Its not my problem that she keeps over-hearing co-workers malicious comments about her weight and that its hurting her so much that she's starving herself in the attempt to get to a super-model size, just so they'll stop." Seriously? He can't say <i>one</i> thing in her defense, even as a friend because the guys might get the impression that he actually has feelings for a woman that doesn't look like a Victoria's Secret model? God, I hated this. By the end of the book I wanted to give Zoe a cookie and tell her to jump ship on this relationship.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11415270795255812780" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Another really funny, over-the-top, steamy HOT <i>Neighbor From Hell</i> romance.</b> IMHO, this was just as good (if not a wee bit better) than Playing for Keeps. <br/> <br/>Trevor wants the PERFECT WIFE:<br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/photos/1330899293p8/447432.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So Trevor is a typical Bradford male, a guy who is completely full of himself and darn right clueless about women, but who is also considerate (when he tries), loyal and sexy as hell.   <span id="freeText17267747573799486234" style="display:none"><br><b>Oh, I loved it! Another really funny, over-the-top, steamy HOT <i>Neighbor From Hell</i> romance.</b> IMHO, this was just as good (if not a wee bit better) than Playing for Keeps. <br> <br>Trevor wants the PERFECT WIFE:<br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/photos/1330899293p8/447432.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Trevor is a typical Bradford male, a guy who is completely full of himself and darn right clueless about women, but who is also considerate (when he tries), loyal and sexy as hell. He could eat you out of house and home, but he is also a hard worker and a devoted family guy who will be there for you in a pinch. <br><br>Trevor:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722754._SY540_.jpg" width="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722755.jpg" width="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Zoe shares a town-home with her landlord’s nephew, a converted building where the top and bottom half are their own units. The walls are thin, the driveway small, but the rent is cheap. And the guy living upstairs is going to drive her insane! So when he steels her pizza delivery on the same day she lost her job and her car window broke, she lets him know what a terrible neighbor he is – only to find out he owns the building (and is her real landlord) and is the biggest jerk alive. <br><br>Zoe:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722756._SY540_.jpg" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722757.jpg" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Feeling like a total cad for insulting Zoe’s weight problem and making her run away crying, he goes about trying to make amends. He helps her get a job at the Bradford’s construction site as the office manager, offers to repair her car, and even offers her a part time job working as his personal shopper and house cleaner. Keeping the refrigerator full might just be the hardest part of her job. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722758._SY540_.jpg" width="120" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722759.jpg" width="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as Zoe starts to get her life back on track, and is even losing weight, she can’t help but feel lonely. And horny. Really horny! So could she really do a friends-with-benefits with her hot neighbor? Why not. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389394641i/8028060._SX540_.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>My final thoughts</b><br>This was such a great addition to the Neighbors From Hell series. I can't wait for the next. I loved Trevor and Zoe, even when he was being a jerk and she was pushing his buttons, they really worked for me. They were smoking hot together too, and I really felt the sexual tension between them. It kept me laughing until the end, and the ending made me a believer in these crazy Bradford guys. <br><br>I think why I might like this one a bit more than Playing For Keep is that Trevor wasn't quite as obnoxious as Jason, and I could relate to so many of their situations. Zoe's weight problem was a big part of this story, and with that comes a woman who doesn't feel beautiful or worthy of a hot guy like Trevor. It does take him a while to see past her weight issue, but I liked that he got to know her as a person first anyway. As he fell for her as a person, his opinion of her body morphed into total desire and wild lust. I also enjoyed the ending in Perfection too as it wasn't overly angsty like in PFK. When he decided Zoe was going to be his, he holds nothing back. You have to love a guy who is willling to go to such lengths for the woman he loves. <i>Sigh</i> <br><br>We also get to see lots more of Jason, Haley and their little rug rats! <br><br>Look! A baby Bradford, ready to chow down:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370004i/722761.jpg" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Perfection</i> was...well, perfection. :-)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11725677261141667005"><blockquote><b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12351649.Perfection__Neighbor_from_Hell___2_' title='Perfection (Neighbor from Hell, #2) by R.L. Mathewson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Perfection</a> is a funny book, with tonnes of good-natured banter and sly flippant humour but as Bill Maher recently discovered, great comedy is a trifecta of timing, content, and delivery.</b>I think we know that even a great comic can and has been derailed by the content of their act. <br/><br/>This book, for me, was let down by Trevor, what with the constant derision of Zoe's looks, hair, weight, clothes etc. Yes, he eventually sees the error of his ways but by which time I had lost all interest.<br/><br/>Oftentimes, I</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11725677261141667005" style="display:none"><blockquote><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12351649.Perfection__Neighbor_from_Hell___2_" title="Perfection (Neighbor from Hell, #2) by R.L. Mathewson" rel="nofollow noopener">Perfection</a> is a funny book, with tonnes of good-natured banter and sly flippant humour but as Bill Maher recently discovered, great comedy is a trifecta of timing, content, and delivery.</b>I think we know that even a great comic can and has been derailed by the content of their act. <br /><br />This book, for me, was let down by Trevor, what with the constant derision of Zoe's looks, hair, weight, clothes etc. Yes, he eventually sees the error of his ways but by which time I had lost all interest.<br /><br />Oftentimes, I found myself laughing <b>AT</b> Trevor rather than with him; just as I felt overwhelmed by the constant reference to the "Bradford appetite for food" or the "Bradford looks" then my favourite, the "Bradford studs". 🙄🔫<br /><br />Oh for the love of all that is holy and snickers ice cream, I wanted to bludgeon someone (preferably myself) but happily, I sailed through with no injuries. To avoid even the possibility of girl slapping myself, I'm refraining from the other books in the series. </blockquote></span>

    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/868141632?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/15777478-perfection">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-r-l-mathewson">author-r-l-mathewson</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=laugh-giggle-snicker-snort">laugh-giggle-snicker-snort</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=sexy-deliciousness">sexy-deliciousness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-neighbor-from-hell">series-neighbor-from-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=sexiest-couples">sexiest-couples</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer868141632" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9730365864614787333"><i>Full review now posted...</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>5 ‘damned near perfect’ stars!!</i>
</b><blockquote>
  <i>"Does no one care that she just manhandled me?" Trevor demanded, facing the men who should be properly outraged on his behalf.<br/><br/>Jason snorted. "As long as brings me food, she can bitch slap you and call you spanky."<br/><br/>Trevor narrowed his eyes on the men who dared laugh at his pain.<br/><br/>Betraying bastards.</i>
</blockquote><i>Perfection</i> is the second book in R.L. Mathewson’s <i>Neighbor From Hell</i> series and again, one helluva funny read. Like the first book, this one</span>
  <span id="freeText9730365864614787333" style="display:none"><i>Full review now posted...</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>5 ‘damned near perfect’ stars!!</i>
</b><blockquote>
  <i>"Does no one care that she just manhandled me?" Trevor demanded, facing the men who should be properly outraged on his behalf.<br /><br />Jason snorted. "As long as brings me food, she can bitch slap you and call you spanky."<br /><br />Trevor narrowed his eyes on the men who dared laugh at his pain.<br /><br />Betraying bastards.</i>
</blockquote><i>Perfection</i> is the second book in R.L. Mathewson’s <i>Neighbor From Hell</i> series and again, one helluva funny read. Like the first book, this one has laugh out loud dialog, romance, holy hell it's hot in here heat, and I couldn’t put it down! <br /><br /><b>Description…</b><br /><br />Zoe is used to taking care of herself and has long ago accepted that if anything bad was going to happen, it was going to happen to her. So when she loses her job over something most bosses would probably be happy with and her life starts going down hill from there she doesn't expect it to get any better. She certainly didn't expect any help from the loud jerk next door, but then again she has nothing to lose so puts her trust in him and hopes for the best. What she didn't expect was the once in a lifetime opportunity that he offers her through an arrangement where they both benefit and no one is supposed to get hurt, but she should have known better because her luck has never been that good.<br /><br />Like most Bradfords, Trevor has a soft spot for food, but that's about all. He leads a pretty straightforward life and likes to keep things simple and that includes his relationships. He wants the perfect woman and knows exactly what she'll be like. So when he discovers much to his horror that he's thinking about his frumpy little neighbor he decides the best way to get his head straight is by working her out of his system. He'll keep her around, but only until he finds perfection.<br /><br /><b>My review…</b><br /><br />At the risk of repeating myself… this is one of the funniest books I’ve ever read. The humor is silly humor, but still laugh out loud comical when you ‘hear’ what’s going through Trevor’s head. At first I was a little put off by the ‘fat’ comments from him and his friends, but the author does a great job of making them look like such moronic douche-waffles that I was actually giggling at their cluelessly callous remarks.<br /><br />And also, just to say… this is one helluva hot story, too. The sexual chemistry between Trevor and Zoe burns up the pages and gives them a spot on my ‘sexiest couple’ shelf that I created with them in mind.<br /><br /><b>The bottom line…</b><br /><br />This isn’t a tragic, compelling, tormented hero read. There are no deep, dark secrets, and no emotional rollercoaster rides. What this is, is a light, sexy romance, and more fun than I can find the words to express. Entertaining, start to finish, and I am soooooooo looking forward to reading more!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9730365864614787333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2562831038" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2562831038" />
    <a title="peachygirl" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/51435362-peachygirl"><img alt="peachygirl" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555561561p2/51435362.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2562831038?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="peachygirl" class="user" itemprop="url" name="peachygirl" href="/user/show/51435362-peachygirl">peachygirl</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/51435362-peachygirl?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2562831038" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14674577805457163533">So Trevor is basically another food obsessed weirdo in the long line of Bradfords and the second neighbor from hell. But unlike Jason, this guy is a jerk who thinks he is God's gift to womenkind and doesn't give a damn about anything except eating and fucking. He keeps bragging (thankfully, in his soliloquy) that he has done a favour to Zoe by asking her to sleep with him. And that he'll only carry on this "arrangement" with his plain, frumpy tenant till he finds the perfect wife for him, who wo</span>
  <span id="freeText14674577805457163533" style="display:none">So Trevor is basically another food obsessed weirdo in the long line of Bradfords and the second neighbor from hell. But unlike Jason, this guy is a jerk who thinks he is God's gift to womenkind and doesn't give a damn about anything except eating and fucking. He keeps bragging (thankfully, in his soliloquy) that he has done a favour to Zoe by asking her to sleep with him. And that he'll only carry on this "arrangement" with his plain, frumpy tenant till he finds the perfect wife for him, who would make every guy around a 10 mile radius burn with jealously and cook like a Master chef contestant. All the while thinking, he'll never be pussy-whipped like his cousin i.e. have loving feelings for his wife. As if this wasn't enough to make me want to give him several swift kicks in his ass, he keeps rambling about how a generous and giving person he is. Such a douche!<br /><br />Zoe, on the other hand was so bloody sweet and deserved better than this miserable jerkwad. I hated how she was body shamed throughout the book and her being so accepting about the whole scenario. Wish she had taken a bat to Trevor's and his buddies' heads and taught them a lesson.<br /><br />Trevor does try to make up for all the shit he put her through, but never does it feel enough. The ending was all sappy and shit like the previous book with food obsessed 'cute' kids and large, happy family gatherings, but there could have been a bit of grovelling for the guy before Zoe agreed to marry his sorry ass. Considering the over the top humor and okayish romance, I'd probably give this book 3 stars. Definitely a let down from Playing for keeps.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14674577805457163533" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283102115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6256751013380083773"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/02/review-perfection-by-r-l-mathewson.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>October 2013 Reread- This book once again rocked my world!!<br/><br/><br/><b>WARNING! Do not read this in public areas...people think you are crazy when you laugh hysterically for seemingly no reason...assholes</b><br/><br/>This has got to be the best 72p I have EVER spent and has now sparked off a teeny tiny obsession with buying every book that R.L. Mathewson has ever published. <br/><br/>Zoe has had the worst day of her life. Ever. Attacked by the bosses wife, unfairly fired from her soul destroying job, her car window breaking a</span>
  <span id="freeText6256751013380083773" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/02/review-perfection-by-r-l-mathewson.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333934i/693541.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>October 2013 Reread- This book once again rocked my world!!<br><br><br><b>WARNING! Do not read this in public areas...people think you are crazy when you laugh hysterically for seemingly no reason...assholes</b><br><br>This has got to be the best 72p I have EVER spent and has now sparked off a teeny tiny obsession with buying every book that R.L. Mathewson has ever published. <br><br>Zoe has had the worst day of her life. Ever. Attacked by the bosses wife, unfairly fired from her soul destroying job, her car window breaking and then the final straw her arrogant neighbour from hell stealing her pick-me-up pizza. She can't take any more. But the confrontation with her neighbour the handsome, arrogant food obsessed Trevor leads in to unexpected directions as they set up a little arrangement to benefit them both.<br><br>I bought this on impulse as I love plain Jane stories, I am ashamed to say I thought it would be a quick enjoyable but ultimately forgettable read, I was wrong, I LOVED this book. It was funny and sexy and it reminded me alot of Shelly Laurenston's style, it has the same foul mouthed, sarcastic humour THAT I LOVE! Trevor also reminded me alot of an SL hero (Briec!) he was adorably arrogant, completely self centered most the time but also hot as hell. Zoe was good as well, funny and I loved seeing her come out her shell, watching her wind up Trevor was hilarious.<br><br>The romance between them as well as being funny, was also sweet and steamy, they slowly went from fuck-buddies to being in a relationship without either of them really noticing. The other characters around them were also great, the whole Bradford Clan were completely food obsessed and a little insane and I can't wait to read more about them!<br><br>This was a great book, I loved every second of it am now off to Amazon to loot the rest of R.L Mathewson's books...!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6256751013380083773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_277370270" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/277370270" />
    <a title="Ana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1316580-ana"><img alt="Ana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491291179p2/1316580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/277370270?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ana" href="/user/show/1316580-ana">Ana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=zz-read-in-2012">zz-read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1316580-ana?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer277370270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10886473548068796237">R.L. Mathewson is quite a find. I'm never quite as grateful for GoodReads as when I love a book, I wouldn't have picked up if not for my friends.<br/><br/>Trevor (cousin of Jason, hero of the first book) is a typical Bradford, meaning he has an unhealthy obsession with food.<br/><br/>But unlike his cousin, he's not as confident. Things were never that easy for him, especially not school. As a matter of fact, since he is dyslexic school was a nightmare of epic proportions. Since he never got to shine, he decided to </span>
  <span id="freeText10886473548068796237" style="display:none">R.L. Mathewson is quite a find. I'm never quite as grateful for GoodReads as when I love a book, I wouldn't have picked up if not for my friends.<br /><br />Trevor (cousin of Jason, hero of the first book) is a typical Bradford, meaning he has an unhealthy obsession with food.<br /><br />But unlike his cousin, he's not as confident. Things were never that easy for him, especially not school. As a matter of fact, since he is dyslexic school was a nightmare of epic proportions. Since he never got to shine, he decided to marry a perfect woman, so that everybody would envy him. She would haven to be stunning, smart, a great cook - basically perfect. And then there's his tenant Zoe. She doesn't fit a single criterium of his. and yet, he can't stop thinking about her.<br /><br />Zoe is aware that she's no man's ideal woman. But she really doesn't need a hunk like Trevor telling her so. She just got fired, she's having quite a bad day, the last thing she needs is her neighbor from hell doing something stupid again. He's impossible! And yet, as she slowly comes to know him, he grows on her.<br /><br />I like this book, but not quite as much as the first one.<br /><br />Zoe is OK, unsure of herself, but still with a great sense of humor and generosity. Trevor himself is not bad, a bit wacky, but mostly great. Except for one thing.<br /><br />The way he thinks of Zoe is a bit disturbing. Calling her fat, unattractive, not worthy of him... REALLY?! It took him a while to realize he's in love with her, mainly because he kept waiting for his PERFECT wife to show up. But this scene made up a bit for his behavior (his "friend" Hank brought him a woman to meet, at that time he's sleeping with Zoe). It's a bit long, but I loved it. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Frowning, Trevor looked back at the woman named Mandy and looked her over. She was beautiful, stunningly so. She had just the right amount of makeup, perfect silky long black hair ending halfway down her back. Her breasts were high and full without the look of plastic and her figure was absolutely perfect.<br /><br />"We thought we'd head back to the girl's place so that Mandy could cook us all dinner. She's a chef," Hank announced with a cocky grin, no doubt knowing how attractive a woman who could cook was to a Bradford.<br /><br />What he didn't know was that so far Mandy was scoring pretty high on Trevor's perfect woman list. He shot a look over his shoulder before stepping out onto the front stoop and closing the door behind him.<br />He shot Mandy a smile that she quickly returned.<br /><br />"So, Mandy, tell me....are you a Yankees fan?"<br /><br />"Yes," she said, giving him a flirty little smile.<br /><br />"Are you close to your family?"<br /><br />"Yes."<br /><br />"Large family?"<br /><br />"Yes," she answered, frowning a bit at his questions or the rapid fire way he was asking them, he didn't know or care.<br /><br />"Do you think you're fat?" he asked, narrowing his eyes on her as he waited for her to answer.<br /><br />Her beautiful, perfectly painted mouth worked soundlessly for a moment before she answered. "A little, but I'm on a diet," she rushed to explain as if that's what he wanted to hear.<br /><br />"Do you like dogs?"<br /><br />"Yes, but I'm more of a cat person."<br /><br />"Are you clingy?" he demanded.<br /><br />"No," she answered with a nervous laugh as she shot her sister, who only shrugged, a look.<br /><br />With a regrettable sigh he shook his head. "I'm sorry, but this isn't going to work out."<br /><br />"What the hell are you doing, Trevor?"<br /><br />Hank demanded anxiously. No doubt the man wouldn't be getting laid tonight, but Trevor couldn't help it. He had his standards and this woman failed them.<br /><br />----------------<br /><br />What the hell was the man thinking bringing a woman like that to meet him? Did the man think he was so desperate that he'd consider sleeping with a woman like that? It was really insulting, he thought as he climbed onto the couch behind Zoe and pulled her back against his body. She of course rewarded him with an elbow to his gut, which he manfully took since she turned in his arms and cuddled up quite nicely against him.<br /><br />A half hour later as he dozed off he wondered why Hank brought him a woman like that when he clearly had standards. Then he remembered that the man was a fucking moron and that explained everything.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />I also liked Toby, Zoe's dog, a German Shepard/Husky mix. He's so cute, and Zoe/Trevor war about what's proper for a male dog to own is adorable.<br /><br />There are actually quite a lot of LOL scenes. I really enjoyed the book, besides Trevor's TSTL moments. :-)<br /><br />I'm definitely going to continue with the series. For all those interested, yes, there will be a next book. :-)<br /><br />Rating:<br /><br /><b>4 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10886473548068796237" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_286038487" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/286038487" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/286038487?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer286038487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3239402765650495293">Perfection is the second book in A Neighbor from Hell series showcasing Jason’s cousin Trevor. I disliked Trevor immensely. He’s boorish, selfish and when it comes to the heroine, Zoe, he treats her poorly. Poor Zoe is a former foster child who has no family and ends up losing her job for doing the right thing. She lives in the same building with Trevor, who’s the landlord. It’s only him and her who live there. He’s a horrible neighbor, both greedy and selfish, only thinking of his own needs, an</span>
  <span id="freeText3239402765650495293" style="display:none">Perfection is the second book in A Neighbor from Hell series showcasing Jason’s cousin Trevor. I disliked Trevor immensely. He’s boorish, selfish and when it comes to the heroine, Zoe, he treats her poorly. Poor Zoe is a former foster child who has no family and ends up losing her job for doing the right thing. She lives in the same building with Trevor, who’s the landlord. It’s only him and her who live there. He’s a horrible neighbor, both greedy and selfish, only thinking of his own needs, and after Zoe gets fired, all she wants to do is eat her pizza she orders. Trevor steals the pizza, because he’s been banned from most restaurants and take out places for some unknown reason. Trevor is scary obsessed with food, and when Zoe confronts him, he says she doesn’t need to eat the pizza, implying she’s fat. Zoe is what you would call a bigger woman weight wise. Trevor then feels guilty for what he has done and offers her a job as his personal housekeeper of sorts and getting her job as his uncle’s secretary.<br /><br />Things are looking up for Zoe and she decides she wants to have more of a social life and that means dating and sex. When Trevor finds out she’s on the prowl for a man, he volunteers to help her out, although they must keep their relationship a secret because she’s not the right woman for him. The fact that she’s overweight and his friends and work buddies will make fun of him makes Trevor wary in letting anyone know what Zoe means to him. Zoe is fine with the friends with benefits thing and Trevor really makes her happy in bed. He’s a big giver and doesn’t mind her curves at all, even as she starve herself to lose weight, which to her surprise Trevor is angry about. Soon Trevor can’t stop thinking about Zoe and wants much more from her. He decides she must stay with him and make him happy until he tires of her, which may be another few decades or so.<br /><br />I have a love/hate relationship with Perfection. It’s pretty much the same tone as Playing for Keeps, but Trevor is a major asshat. My dislike for him grew during one scene when his co-workers are making fun of Zoe’s weight and calling her rude names. Trevor allows it because he feels if he comes to her defense, they’ll figure out he has feelings for her and in turn make fun of him. There were many instances where Trevor would put down Zoe in his mind while wanting to have sex with her every which way. Toward the end he was somewhat redeemed, but he’s pretty much selfish until the end. Also the non-stop obsession with food for him and the amount he eats is so over the top and unrealistic. Zoe has very little backbone and I felt so bad for her, even though she has many orgasms thanks to Trevor.<br /><br />I was at odds with Perfection overall because it was too zany and Trevor is just too selfish and I wanted to chuck him over a cliff. But even with my issues with Trevor, I did enjoy this one but with some reservations.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3239402765650495293" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_281019708" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/281019708" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/281019708?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=spunky-heroine">spunky-heroine</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer281019708" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11538568388252294954">A delightful, crazy romp with another food obsessed, bossy, obnoxious Bradford. This book had me laughing out loud at all Trevor’s crazy antics. What a scrumptious nut job. Zoe needs someone to be her champion and Trevor is just the man for the job. She’s his tenant and they’ve never spoken, but he still manages to annoy the HELL out of her. The first time they have a face to face encounter he insults her, over food of course, and regrets what he says the minute it comes out of his mouth. So, he</span>
  <span id="freeText11538568388252294954" style="display:none">A delightful, crazy romp with another food obsessed, bossy, obnoxious Bradford. This book had me laughing out loud at all Trevor’s crazy antics. What a scrumptious nut job. Zoe needs someone to be her champion and Trevor is just the man for the job. She’s his tenant and they’ve never spoken, but he still manages to annoy the HELL out of her. The first time they have a face to face encounter he insults her, over food of course, and regrets what he says the minute it comes out of his mouth. So, he tries to right the wrong by helping her out and along the way, he falls in love with her. <br><br>See, Zoe’s a plump girl, and Trevor has a list of standards that his future wife needs to meet. Zoe meets none of them, but it doesn’t matter, because even though in Trevor’s head she’s not perfect, his heart has him feeling differently…only it takes him FOREVER to realize it. I cracked up as Trevor kept convincing himself that she is nothing that he wants, but being he’s such a “giver”, this is what drives him to take care of her. He also helps satisfy her sexual needs, his way of protecting her from all the evil men out there who will just take advantage of her...yeah right Trevor!!! Oh and the two of them were insatiable, and did “it” six ways to Sunday…very HOT! Zoe held her own against Trevor and as much as he played her, she played him right back. They interacted so well and made an amusing couple.<br><br>Initially I thought that since the first book ended 10 years in the future that this book would continue from that point. What a pleasant surprise, when I realized that it was only 2 years later and that Haley and Jason were expecting their second child. So, not only did we get Trevor and Zoe’s story, we got crazy Jason and the lovely Haley too. Jason hasn’t changed much and fatherhood has made him nuttier and even more arrogant, didn’t think THAT was possible, but he is. When Jason and Trevor were together it was like Laurel and Hardy on testosterone. Food is what drives this family and they ate so much I started to get a stomachache, although I think some of it was from laughing so much. <br><br>Just another fun well-written book from this talented author, with witty dialogue, crazy antics and charming loveable characters! <br><br><a href="http://s1130.photobucket.com/albums/m524/kparks823/?action=view&amp;current=bradfordatabuffet-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380370359i/723172._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>We are currently having a Giveaway at Swept Away By Romance-R.L. Mathewson is giving away ALL of her published books to 2 very lucky winners (ends on February 23, 2012)</b> <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/">http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/</a><br></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=she-is-pregnant">she-is-pregnant</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1905698290" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7616927734848024408"><b>This was shockingly a huge disappointment</b> of something that could have been very good. I adore friends to lovers books, adore it even more when they start off as enemies... however I hate it when the characters ruins what could've been a good story. Though not much happened in this book, it would still be interesting enough to enjoy if it weren't for the characters. I didn't mind <b>Zoe O'Shea</b> (29) so much, simply because she was a plain character (ironic, really, considering that's how our male ch</span>
  <span id="freeText7616927734848024408" style="display:none"><b>This was shockingly a huge disappointment</b> of something that could have been very good. I adore friends to lovers books, adore it even more when they start off as enemies... however I hate it when the characters ruins what could've been a good story. Though not much happened in this book, it would still be interesting enough to enjoy if it weren't for the characters. I didn't mind <b>Zoe O'Shea</b> (29) so much, simply because she was a plain character (ironic, really, considering that's how our male character found her as a woman) and you just wouldn't mind her as she just is. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We all fuck up when it comes to our women and you will too. The key is to make her love you more than you piss her off,” Jason added. “It’s a very delicate balance.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Trevor Bradford</b> (30+?) on the other hand... damn, I can't tell you how many times I wanted to slap his face, roll my eyes, or stab him. He was not just arrogant (I don't mind an arrogant man, but there's a line, and if you cross it...big no), he was rude, mean and weak. If you know me, then you know the male character is a <i>huge</i> deal to me. <b>If I don't like the man</b>, then the book is over for me. I simply <i>need</i> to love the male character in a book. It's just that simple. Though Trevor pick himself up in the end, it didn't make up for all the shit he did for the rest of the book. He had his cute moments, but for the most part, I really disliked him. Might even had hated him at some point. So overall, the story got destroyed because of the characters, aka Trevor. Also, I wasn't a fan of the food 'issue' the people had in this book...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She also wasn’t the type of woman who made men drool, besides him, and got the attention of every guy in the room, but that was okay because none of them should be fucking looking at her anyway.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486501698i/21921306.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Toby and Max<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - I'm stupid, who knows.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - No, not really.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 2 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText10319062362634685467" style="display:none">Trevor Bradford has his ideal wife in mind and she is perfect from head to toe, in fact he has a list with the traits that they need to possess in order to maintain perfection. His quiet little tenant in his townhouse has a few of those traits but she is hardly his type and she is a full figured woman and his plans to have a svelte wife who cooks like a goddess is more important.<br /><br />Zoe has had it with her neighbor, he is loud, dirty, and inconsiderate. After the day from hell where she promptly lost her job after uncovering a thief, she had car troubles and is a sopping wet mess due to the weather. What she really needs is comfort food and to curl up in a ball, what she gets is her neighbor stealing her takeout order and insulted all in the same breath.<br /><br />What starts out as a tolerable relationship ends up leading to a friends with benefits but no commitment arrangement, but to think it will be easy to maintain a distance is proving to be harder than both of them thought.<br /><br />I would have given this a five, but Trevor is a bit of a dick for awhile. He is funny and charming in his own weird way but it took him awhile to man up. However I give this a 4.75 I was laughing out loud repeatedly, the Bradfords and their food habits crack me up. Great book.</span>

    <a title="Mimi Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith"><img alt="Mimi Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297016674p2/4884889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/276293876?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12983777-perfection">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4884889-mimi-smith?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer276293876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13896113452503491957"><b>3 stars</b><br/><br/>Another great installment in the series! A really fun book. <br/><br/>So, we're back with the Bradfords and their food obsession. This time the dastardly neighbor is Trevor, Jason's cousin. His little tenant is Zoe. <br/><br/>Zoe has had a bad day/year/life. She's survived foster care, a shitty job and termination. She is now jobless and pissed off. And she will not let her neighbor still her food too! She is an interesting character. Really smart, but with a low, low self-esteem, because she is overweight, </span>
  <span id="freeText13896113452503491957" style="display:none"><b>3 stars</b><br /><br />Another great installment in the series! A really fun book. <br /><br />So, we're back with the Bradfords and their food obsession. This time the dastardly neighbor is Trevor, Jason's cousin. His little tenant is Zoe. <br /><br />Zoe has had a bad day/year/life. She's survived foster care, a shitty job and termination. She is now jobless and pissed off. And she will not let her neighbor still her food too! She is an interesting character. Really smart, but with a low, low self-esteem, because she is overweight, she has a hard time accepting compliments...<br /><br /><i>"You're beautiful, Zoe," he said, realizing at that moment just how beautiful she really was. From her beautiful soft brown hair to her stubborn little chin she was beautiful.<br />"No, I'm not," she said with a snort and an eye roll as she averted her eyes. <br />His eyes narrowed dangerously on her. "Are you calling me a liar?"<br />"More like delusional," she said with a snort.<br />"How dare you question my taste, woman?" he demanded. "If I say you're beautiful then you're beautiful so get the hell over it!" he snapped.<br />"Look, I appreciate the compliment, but-"<br />"Out," he said, dropping onto his back and folding his arms over his chest as he stubbornly looked away from her.<br />"But-"<br />"I said out, woman!"<br />"This is my apartment," Zoe pointed out, sounding close to laughing.<br />"Then you know where the door is. Now get out, woman, and don't you dare come back until you're ready to apologize to me," he said, waving a dismissive hand in the direction of the door.</i><br /><br />I did like how the extreme dieting that Zoe is doing is not portrayed as ok. Trevor actually sees and comments it's wrong for her to starve herself. Other than a very, very assholish comment at the start he doesn't try to belittle her or make her feel less.<br /><br />Trevor is unbelievably arrogant. Kind of like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10790516.Lothaire__Immortals_After_Dark___12_" title="Lothaire (Immortals After Dark, #12) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Lothaire</a>, but without the excuse of being a millenia old vampire. He can do no wrong and the little people are around so they can feed him. For his wife he wants perfection and Zoe is not perfect, so... I had a problem with his thoughts at a certain point. Thinking she's not in his league(not pretty enough) is just wrong all around. Still, it was sweet watching him become the Adoring Disciple of Zoe. The Bradford obsession with food and Trevor's arrogance (which is a consequence of an unhappy childhood) are scary...<br /><br /><i>"Of course he could order food, except for the fact that he was still on the banned list for most of the delivery places.<br />Bastards."<br /><br />"He'd never had a problem convincing anyone that doing something for him was actually to their benefit."<br /><br />""I.....don't want......you," she said, sucking in a breath. "Go...away."<br />Instead of getting mad, which under normal circumstances he probably would have done, he leaned over and pressed a kiss to the back of one of the hands that was holding her head tightly. If he didn't know that she had a head injury and was obviously out of it, he might have taken that personally, but he knew she loved him.<br />How could she not? He was so damn giving after all, he thought as he ducked out of the way before her blind swing could connect with his jaw."</i><br /><br />I loved this book, but I preferred the first one. Trevor's disparaging thoughts, her low self-esteem and the friends with benefits storyline lessened my enjoyment a bit. Still, a great read.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13896113452503491957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer274191574" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8321088140563430450">Funny, hot read, that I couldn't put down. It is my favorite so far between the two of the series and I am glad to see there will be third one. This storyline clicked more with me because it stirred up some good emotions. My heart broke for Zoe with all the demeaning comments she heard about her looks and weight and that she accepted that she wasn't good enough for Trevor. It sort of bummed me out that he didn't stick up for her even as her friend. Trevor was easy to warm up to though and the ve</span>
  <span id="freeText8321088140563430450" style="display:none">Funny, hot read, that I couldn't put down. It is my favorite so far between the two of the series and I am glad to see there will be third one. This storyline clicked more with me because it stirred up some good emotions. My heart broke for Zoe with all the demeaning comments she heard about her looks and weight and that she accepted that she wasn't good enough for Trevor. It sort of bummed me out that he didn't stick up for her even as her friend. Trevor was easy to warm up to though and the verbal interactions between the two had me smiling and chuckling through out. I knew soon as Trevor stated his list of what his future wife's requirements were that it was going to be fun watching him fall madly in love with his future wife's complete opposite.<br /><br />The Bradford men were once again over the top with their food consumption issues, a little silly or too much at times, but some good laughs as they passed that gene to their off springs. Trevor did have some of those jerk tendencies that I love and Zoe ripped them away eventually. Trevor had a little bit of Tate Jackson from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11227040.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a> in him, especially how he belittled Zoe for her looks and weight. He demanded that she would see things his way, he thought he was a god, which I believe he had some godlike qualities and he was beyond arrogant. Trevor also channeled a little bit of Bobby Tom's personality from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73084.Heaven__Texas__Chicago_Stars___2_" title="Heaven, Texas (Chicago Stars, #2) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Heaven, Texas</a>, thinking he was doing Zoe a favor by being with her because he was so much better than her. He tried to manipulate her and finally she cracked him.<br /><br />I also loved seeing Jason and Haley. I am still laughing when Zoe first meets Jason and he is calling sexual harassment. She didn't know what to make of all the crazy Bradford men. <br /><br />I like this author. She is good at making you laugh, gives some some good anticipation anxiety, makes you tingling with the heat she puts in her sex scenes, and I like that her epilogues gives glimpses years out about how wonderful life is with the characters.<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8321088140563430450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText2403032710946010879" style="display:none">Spoiler Free Review<br />4.5 STARS our of 5<br />Genre: Contemporary Romance-Comedy<br /><br /><b>The day from <i>HELL</i></b><br /> Zoe is having the day from <i>HELL</i>. After recovering a trail that extends back six years for embezzlement of funds at her job. She finds herself on the receiving end of unemployment. Huh??? Shouldn't her boss be grateful??? Well one would think so. Oh, but wait that's nothing because her termination comes after she gets an ice latte thrown at her by the embezzler. Once Zoe arrives home she notices that once again her neighbor's truck has taken up both spots in the driveway. Leaving her to park on the street and now be at risk of getting a ticket from the cops. AGAIN.<br />And then at the end of a very taxing day Zoe receives help from the last person she would have ever expected it from. Trevor Bradford. Her A-hole of a neighbor who I must mention has already stolen from her twice already just on that day alone.<i> Her</i> day from<i> HELL</i><br /><br /><b>Looking for Perfection</b><br />Trevor Bradford has that unbelievable appetite possessed by all the Bradford men. If you have read book one in this series then you are aware that he as well as all Bradford men has a bottomless stomach. He works for his uncle who is more like a father figure and plans to marry the<b> perfect</b> woman. A woman who is beautiful with the<b> PERFECT</b> height, shape and can cook her ass off among other things men crave of course. For now he will settle for what he gets until <b>
  <i>Perfection</i>
</b> comes along. As of today Trevor fears he may lose his<b> perfect</b> tenant after a conversation they share where she lets him know she may soon need to move since she has lost her job. But he can't have that...Zoe is the only one who met his requirements as a tenant. So he offers her a gig since he knows his uncle is hiring then he sets her up with a way to earn extra cash by working for him.<br /><br /><b>Friends with Benefits</b> <br />Soon an unexpected friendship blossoms. Then one night everything changes when Zoe goes to a bar to hunt for a man. A girl has needs too! She has been on a dry spell and is in need for sex. YES the girl is horny!lol!! Trevor ends up at the same bar when he spots a drunken Zoe and makes her an offer she can't refuse. Friendship becomes lust and lust turns in to love.<br /><br /><u>Thoughts</u><br />This book was just as hilarious as the first I cannot wait for book three in this series! I recommend this series to all book lovers!!!<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Lovable<br />Writing Style- Favorable. My preferred cup of tea!<br />Plot/Storyline- Good<br />Steam Factor- Medium/Moderately Steamy<br />Overall- I loved it!!!!<br /><br /><b> Now go forth and read.   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/272183486?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer272183486" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8634036366454442687">Five Perfect Stars :)<br/><br/><b>
  <i>As long as she brings me food she can bitch slap you and call you spanky ~ Jason Bradford </i>
</b><br/><br/>I just had to include that quote simply because it made me laugh and it strongly describes how fixated the Bradford men are with food. Its ridiculously hilarious. Though Jason and Haley from the first novel, <i>Playing For Keeps</i>, makes several appearances in this story, this story involved another Bradford family member, Trevor and his shy and sweet tenant, Zoe. Once again, I could not</span>
  <span id="freeText8634036366454442687" style="display:none">Five Perfect Stars :)<br /><br /><b>
  <i>As long as she brings me food she can bitch slap you and call you spanky ~ Jason Bradford </i>
</b><br /><br />I just had to include that quote simply because it made me laugh and it strongly describes how fixated the Bradford men are with food. Its ridiculously hilarious. Though Jason and Haley from the first novel, <i>Playing For Keeps</i>, makes several appearances in this story, this story involved another Bradford family member, Trevor and his shy and sweet tenant, Zoe. Once again, I could not put down this book and finished it in one sitting. I related a lot to Zoe's character and found myself rooting for her from the very beginning. I wanted nothing but good things for her. Enter Trevor. He's her landlord and never had any interest in Zoe and her <i>frumpiness</i>. <br /><br />Trevor is determined to find his idealistic woman, his perfect woman. He has a strict criteria of what he's looking for and Zoe is far from meeting that criteria. However, after putting his foot in his mouth after Zoe has a day from hell, Trevor feels the need to help her. Soon they come to an arrangement of sorts. It starts out as an innocent arrangement, but as things progressed between them, they start a not-so-innocent arrangement. Though this new arrangement is mutually beneficial and the terms are clearly laid down in the beginning, they start to develop an unbreakable relationship. They both strongly deny it at first, but it was inevitable that they were made for each other. It made for a fantastic read. <br /><br />There were SEVERAL times I laughed out loud and felt heartache. The buffet scene had me laughing. Bradfords and buffets is a recipe for disaster. When they get word that a new buffet was opening in town, they all gathered together, but none of them sit together. Why? <i>"Because if one of them is going to get banned today and if we're not careful he'll take us all down with him"</i>. So fabulously funny. <br /><br />Love, love, LOVED this story. The author is brilliant and I can't wait until the next <i>Neighbor from Hell</i> installment comes out. I can't get enough of these Bradford men. =)</span>
  <a data-text-id="8634036366454442687" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17005936039475354954"><b>
  <i>"Would it have killed you to keep it a secret between us?" Trevor asked as they stepped in line. <br/> "It's a buffet Trevor. They would have found out about it within a week," Zoe replied. <br/>"Yes, but that would have been a week that I could have enjoyed this place before those greedy bastards got us all banned." Trevor sighed. <br/> "Gee, I hadn't thought of that," she mumbled, trying not to laugh. <br/>Trevor slowly looked down at her. His eyes narrowed dangerously on her as she did her best to bite back t</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17005936039475354954" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Would it have killed you to keep it a secret between us?" Trevor asked as they stepped in line. <br /> "It's a buffet Trevor. They would have found out about it within a week," Zoe replied. <br />"Yes, but that would have been a week that I could have enjoyed this place before those greedy bastards got us all banned." Trevor sighed. <br /> "Gee, I hadn't thought of that," she mumbled, trying not to laugh. <br />Trevor slowly looked down at her. His eyes narrowed dangerously on her as she did her best to bite back the smile, but lost that battle several times. <br />"Oh my god.... You sold me out!" he said looking shocked. <br /> "I wanted to see how a whole family gets banned from a restaurant" she admitted with a shrug.</i>
</b> <br /><br /><br />OH MAN!! After meeting the Bradfords in the last book I LOVED THAT SCENE! like seriously <b>LOST MY SHIT!</b> Laughing soooo much! If you have read this book you know what I'm talking about.. How everyone is the enemy.. the girls have books... I'm pissing myself laughing just thinking about it! If you haven't read this book PLEASE DO even if its just for that part! <b>TRUST </b> me you will love it! <br /><br />Anywhooo.... <br /><br />This is the story of Trevor and Zoe... Trevor is a Bradford so we do see Hayley and Jason pop in and find out what they are up too. Like when Jason trys to have Hayley fired for sexual harrassment?! LOL... <br /><br />Anyway.. <br />Zoe and Trevor actually live next door to each other. So in True chick lit they hate each other. Until one day they don't... It is your typical friends with benefits turned to lovers turned to HEA. but the ride there was fun. <br />In typical style the author has us laughing, but also being serious when needed. <br /><br />A good little series that I'm glad I came accross. <br /><br />Oh and how funny was her reading him "Twilght" through the walls?! and telling him the sex was coming? LOL I liked Zoe alot... </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LX0657kV9shI+6Mgx8J6xNC14aq7KMdl3M0spnRh/joCKUfGcYtkwg9o5xwr1AKWd1npmjmsumuH6+pgmweetQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SAcYufhXW6gDVz18KCsbUtN8MDRn4Wgckek5dd0TWxBnU2WYMMnJokTEeUDEPWMAdJA4BOVlFRLKz/+zMnU7nw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7724165331247801740">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br/><br/>Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast </span>
  <span id="freeText7724165331247801740" style="display:none">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br /><br />Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast food cook, and a museum worker until she decided to take an EMT course. Working as an EMT helped her get over her shyness as well as left her with some fond memories and some rather disturbing ones that from time to time show up in one of her books. <br /><br />Today, R.L. Mathewson is the single mother of two children that keep her on her toes. She has a bit of a romance novel addiction as well as a major hot chocolate addiction and on a perfect day, she combines the two. <br /><br />In 2019/2020, R.L. Mathewson will be publishing Devastated, the first Anger Management novel, Tall, Dark &amp; Furious, the 6th installment to the Pyte/Sentinel series, Irresistible, the long anticipated novel for the Neighbor from Hell Series as well as many more books throughout the year, paranormals, contemporaries, and YAs. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7724165331247801740" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
